    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

  <span id="freeText17773777677895706426" style="display:none">At thirty-three Warner Truman is one of the richest men on the planet, a spa mogul who buys and sells resorts at will. He holds powerful executive’s careers in his well-groomed hands. Nothing is beyond Warner’s reach…until he meets <i>her.</i><br /><br />Stunning, tantalizing, and perverse, Taddy Brill captivates Warner’s carnal desire like no woman he’s ever met. A self-made millionaire, Taddy is tougher than steel, more brilliant than diamonds and, at twenty-seven, she’s never depended on a man for anything…until she meets <i>him.</i><br /><br />The more Taddy plays with Warner’s affections, driving him to erotic heights, the more she is confronted by a dark past. But before she can love him, Taddy must meet her worst fears head-on or risk losing it all, including herself.<br /><br /><i>A Romantica® contemporary erotic romance from Ellora's Cave</i></span>

<div id="review_685529628" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/685529628" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/685529628?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=arc-or-netgalley">arc-or-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer685529628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14950496299306644493"><br/>♦ <b>4.5 FUN, ENTERTAINING, FABULICIOUS STARS.</b> ♦<br/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431736ra/866558.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  <br/>
</p><blockquote>
  <i>"<b>Manhattanites</b> are noted as a jaded bunch. We own designer footwear in excess, overspend on vodka cocktails and work sunup to sundown. By accident love takes a backseat but we always find time for sex (wink)."</i>
</blockquote><br/><b>FABULOUS. GLAMOUROUS. UNSCRUPULOUS.</b> That's what The Manhattanites are, their lives are full of fame, fashion, glamour, and hard work. Just like the first part of this series, Unscrupulous can be best described as "fun erotica", with mo</span>
  <span id="freeText14950496299306644493" style="display:none"><br>♦ <b>4.5 FUN, ENTERTAINING, FABULICIOUS STARS.</b> ♦<br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431736ra/866558.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
</p><blockquote>
  <i>"<b>Manhattanites</b> are noted as a jaded bunch. We own designer footwear in excess, overspend on vodka cocktails and work sunup to sundown. By accident love takes a backseat but we always find time for sex (wink)."</i>
</blockquote><br><b>FABULOUS. GLAMOUROUS. UNSCRUPULOUS.</b> That's what The Manhattanites are, their lives are full of fame, fashion, glamour, and hard work. Just like the first part of this series, Unscrupulous can be best described as "fun erotica", with moments that will make you want to *fan yourself* and others that will leave you laughing uncontrollably. It reminded me of Sex and the City, but with a sexier edge to it.<br><br><b>Unscrupulous</b> is the second part of The Manhattanites series and tells the story of Taddy Brill, Lex Easton's best friend who already had a brief but memorable introduction in the first part of the series, <i>Undressed</i>. Although this is the second part of the series, this story can easily be read as a standalone. In my opinion, <i>Unscrupulous</i> had a very different vibe from <i>Undressed</i> and I ended up enjoying it even more than Lex's story!<br><br><br>First, let me introduce you to the "hero" of the story: CEO <b>Warner Truman</b>, third richest man of the world.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431736i/866559._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I used to strive to live my life for happiness, not money or status. I don't know what happened or why I stopped."</i>
</blockquote><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/549438.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/551279.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, before you start thinking Warner must be another dominant, controlling billionaire like Christian Grey and Gideon Cross, I can assure you he's <i>nothing</i> like any of them. He doesn't have any dark secrets in his closet, hidden playrooms or other controlling tendencies. He's intelligent, charming and the perfect gentleman, but when he wants something, he's not afraid to go after it. ;-)<br><br>You would think that with a swoonworthy hero like Warner, there would be no doubt about who my favorite character in the story would be, BUT with a heroine like Taddy that isn't exactly the case... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431736i/866560._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></p><blockquote>
  <i>"It's not my intention to be a diva. It just happens. I wake up like I'm flippin' Beyoncé or something."</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431736i/866561.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Taddy Brill</b> is the CEO of Brill, Inc., New York's most elite and succesful public relations company. She's a self-made woman who strives every day to be the best at what she does. She's strong, determined, merciless and never afraid to speak her mind. She's a perfectionist, an obsessive masturbator and a workaholic all at the same time. Estranged from her family, her friends are as close to family as she has and with a busy schedule like hers, there isn't much time for love or relationships.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I never meet men with any expectations other than having a good time. Then I 'm never disappointed."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>But then she meets <b>Warner Truman</b>. A man who has suffered loss and heartbreak in his past as well and who has decided to never again date a woman who's only after his money. Like Taddy, he's a self-made man and that's why he seems to have found a perfect match in her. Both of them know what it's like to built a career from the ground up, they're both powerful and succesful in their business and that creates an immediate bond between them.<br><br>The chemistry between Warner and Taddy is off the charts hot and from the moment they first meet, there's an instant connection between them. As they start to get to know each other better, their feelings start to grow more and more, and they realize how perfectly they complement each other. But will they be able to admit their true feelings to both themselves and each other?<br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I knew I was in love when I couldn't fall asleep because she was lying next to me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>But will they be able to make it work? <br><br>Will their busy scedules and past experiences allow them to open up their hearts and make themselves vulnerable?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431736i/866562.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Aside from Taddy and Warner there were several side characters that made the story all the more colourful and fun to read like Kiki, Taddy's timid assistant, and Taddy's best friends Lex, Vive and Blake. Each one of them has their own unique personnality and the conversations between Taddy and her friends seriously made me laugh-out-loud quite a few times and I'm already looking forward to Vive and Blake's own story!<br><br><br><b>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431736i/866563.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Overall, I think it's safe to say <i>Unscrupulous</i> is one of the funniest, most entertaining books I've read this year and I would highly recommend anyone looking for a sexy, unique read with a healthy dose of humor to give it a try!</b><br><br><br><i>**ARC courtesy of Ellora's Cave via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review**</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14950496299306644493" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/692846296?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13742215-destini-mia?shelf=arc">arc</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692846296" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13246505047835749722"><b>Gear up ladies because Warner is here to grab you by the ovaries!! Resistance is futile. <br/><br/>This book was just… </b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432781ra/870473.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <u>FABULOUS</u>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>Warner, <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432781ra/870474.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Tabitha Adelaide Brillford</b><br/><i>
  <blockquote> “It’s not my intention to be a diva. It just happens. I wake up like I’m flippin’ Beyoncé or something.” </blockquote>
</i><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432781i/870475.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432781i/870476.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Warner Truman</b><br/><blockquote>
  <i> “I used to strive to live my life for happiness, not money or status. I don't know what happened or why I stopped.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432781i/870477._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432781i/870478._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Taddy Brill has always known that the one person she can always count on is herself. She’s be</span>
  <span id="freeText13246505047835749722" style="display:none"><b>Gear up ladies because Warner is here to grab you by the ovaries!! Resistance is futile. <br><br>This book was just… </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432781ra/870473.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>FABULOUS</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Warner, <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432781ra/870474.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Tabitha Adelaide Brillford</b><br><i>
  <blockquote> “It’s not my intention to be a diva. It just happens. I wake up like I’m flippin’ Beyoncé or something.” </blockquote>
</i><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432781i/870475.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432781i/870476.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Warner Truman</b><br><blockquote>
  <i> “I used to strive to live my life for happiness, not money or status. I don't know what happened or why I stopped.”</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432781i/870477._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432781i/870478._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Taddy Brill has always known that the one person she can always count on is herself. She’s been independent since she was sixteen and built her PR empire from the ground up. She doesn’t depend on anyone, that way nobody has a chance to let her down. So when “Big Daddy” Warner comes along, she treats him like all the others, even though she knows he’s different. Her walls are staying up, just where they belong. But Warner is not taking no for an answer… <br><br><i>Unscrupulous</i> was a fun, entertaining, and yummy read that I couldn’t put down for a second! The writing was easy, but captivating and I didn’t want to tear my eyes away from the magic *wink*. <br><br>As fun and just all out fabulous these two characters were, they haven’t had a perfectly paved out life. <br>Taddy lived the high life as a child. Her parents had their problems but she never expected that she’d have their love taken away from her. My heart <i>hurt</i> for Taddy. That prologue just gutted me because you could <b>feel</b> how confused and heartbroken she was. <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <i><blockquote> “You could still act as if she’s your daughter,” her mother cried. <br>“She’s not.”</blockquote></i><br><br>That just broke my heart.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432781i/870479._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Warner has also gone through some really tough situations and it just made me love him more. This sexy, man beast and his soft side captured my heart. <br><br>How I <b>loved</b> Taddy!! Her personality and <i>being</i> kept me laughing in shock throughout the whole book. That pedicure scene <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[with the chair <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> had me on the floor laughing. Poor guy… <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432781ra/870480.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Unscrupulous</i> is a book I’d recommend for anybody in need of a hilarious, sexy time read!<br>Now onto Lex’s story and my prince charming… <br><br><i>**ARC courtesy of the author via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review**</i><br><br>__________________________________________<br><b>More of my Manhattanites reviews:<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/694541323" rel="nofollow noopener">Undressed (The Manhattanites, #1)</a><br>______________________________________<br></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_695201665" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/695201665" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/695201665?book_show_action=true">Aug 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer695201665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6645040288086533770"><a href='http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/Emotions/worshipping_zps255e0bd7.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/638931.gif' alt=' photo worshipping_zps255e0bd7.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>4.5 laugh-out-loud stars! <br/><br/>If you're looking for a light-hearted, funny, breath-of-fresh-air read, this one delivers in spades! Thank you Avery for breaking my book funk! Taddy was the PERFECT heroine!<br/><br/>Unscrupulous is written with a witty, sassy dialect that kept my attention combined with steamy hot, albeit comical at times, sex scenes. <br/><br/><b>Manhattanites are noted as a jaded bunch. We own designer footwear in excess, overspend on vodka cocktails and work sunup to sundown. By accident love takes a</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6645040288086533770" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/Emotions/worshipping_zps255e0bd7.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/638931.gif" alt=" photo worshipping_zps255e0bd7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>4.5 laugh-out-loud stars! <br><br>If you're looking for a light-hearted, funny, breath-of-fresh-air read, this one delivers in spades! Thank you Avery for breaking my book funk! Taddy was the PERFECT heroine!<br><br>Unscrupulous is written with a witty, sassy dialect that kept my attention combined with steamy hot, albeit comical at times, sex scenes. <br><br><b>Manhattanites are noted as a jaded bunch. We own designer footwear in excess, overspend on vodka cocktails and work sunup to sundown. By accident love takes a backseat but we always find time for sex (wink)."</b><br><br>Taddy Brill is an uber successful Manhattanite, owning her own company with the help of her very gay, unhappily married friend Blake (can't wait for his book btw). Sorry to digress.... Taddy has close friendships with Lex and Vive, also very successful businesswomen. Their lives are about a lot of work, drinks, and singledom (is that a word?). Taddy has no functional family to speak of...being an emancipated minor, she's worked hard for where she is and her friends are her family. She's uber loyal and will do anything for them in times of need.<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/image_zps3abb3e0f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433109i/871389._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps3abb3e0f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Warner Truman is a widower, very private and doesn't date much since a betrayal of his ex fiancée. He's the third richest man in the world and has worked hard for where he's at. When he runs into this stunning redhead at his St Barths resort, sparks fly. He hasn't felt this pull towards a woman in years.... They get acquainted over champagne talk.<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/image_zpsfb3b88e0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433109i/871390._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsfb3b88e0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/ladyboner_zps8e242efa.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399664ra/773693.gif" alt=" photo ladyboner_zps8e242efa.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Taddy hasn't been told "I love you" ever in life. Not from parents, not from friends. Regardless of her profound loyalty, she's very guarded to accept any man's affections beyond sex. She's been rejected in the worst way as a child and those scars run deep. Warner sparks something in her she WANTS to pursue but can she take a chance with him?<br><br>What did I love about this book, you say? The cast of characters, especially Taddy. She's got insecurity issues but she's a tough broad and doesn't wallow in self pity. Hallelujah to a strong heroine. She drops anything to aide her friends and dominates the business sector. What a breath of fresh air! Awesome! Loved Taddy!<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/BFF_zps3cf06e42.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433109ra/871391.gif" alt=" photo BFF_zps3cf06e42.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> Then there's Warner, sexy beast that he is. Love, love, love that he's all alpha strong, successful, rich, and doesn't have a shit-ton of secrets in his closet.... Another common "trait" of late in erotic novels... Weak heroines, rich men with secrets. Nope, not here. It was refreshing to see a relationship with a fair share of baggage but both people approaching it maturely. Some of their antics and "issues" in bed were comical yet true to life. He's a talker....she's not. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/General%20erotic%20stuff/makingoutbed_zps075fe695.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433109ra/871392.gif" alt=" photo makingoutbed_zps075fe695.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book has serious laugh out loud moments. It wasn't forced, just flowed with the personality of this crew. It has a very Sex in the City feel to it. And we all know who Mr Big is in this book....<br><br>.<a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/penis_zps0861806a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/623726.gif" alt=" photo penis_zps0861806a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Looking SO forward to Blake, Vive, and Sheldon's books! Hint hint. Sheldon....Warner's tattooed badboy little brother..swoon. Some of my favorite quotes.....<br><br>Taddy getting a pedicure......<br><b>"“Please do not masturbate while I do your feet. I cannot take another moaning horny white woman this week.”</b><br><br>Taddy-<br><b>"I'm a perfectionist. I'm also an obsessive masturbator, a workaholic, and I started smoking again. </b><br><br>Taddy talking about when she had Mononucleosis-<br><b>"I had lymph nodes the size of grapefruits...and my enlarged spleen caused constant abdominal pain. My skin had gone jaundiced." So yellow she could've passed for Laa-Laa the yellow Teletubby.</b><br><br>Thanks Avery Aster for the opportunity to read your brilliance and provide my HONEST review! You're the shizzle!<br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/Emotions/sosweet_zpsda653eda.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425589i/849499.jpg" alt=" photo sosweet_zpsda653eda.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6645040288086533770" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692137555" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17833943108370551406"><i> ARC provided by Netgalley </i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432678i/869372._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432678ra/869373.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432678i/869374._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432678i/869375._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432678i/869376.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432678i/869377.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"May I?<br/><br/>"You may."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>For those of us who missed <i>Sex and the City</i> and crave a strong willed & sassy Heroine look no further than Miss <b>Tabitha "Taddy Brill" Adelaine Brillford.</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432678ra/869378.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>A girl who had everything and lost everything because of the choices her parents made. Seriously many people should really not have kids... *snip, snip* you know what I'm saying?<br/><br/>From the first page I was <b>IN LOVE</b>.. and not only because it's set in </span>
  <span id="freeText17833943108370551406" style="display:none"><i> ARC provided by Netgalley </i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432678i/869372._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432678ra/869373.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432678i/869374._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432678i/869375._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432678i/869376.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432678i/869377.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"May I?<br><br>"You may."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>For those of us who missed <i>Sex and the City</i> and crave a strong willed &amp; sassy Heroine look no further than Miss <b>Tabitha "Taddy Brill" Adelaine Brillford.</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432678ra/869378.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A girl who had everything and lost everything because of the choices her parents made. Seriously many people should really not have kids... *snip, snip* you know what I'm saying?<br><br>From the first page I was <b>IN LOVE</b>.. and not only because it's set in my stomping ground - NYC.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432678ra/869379.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> A hilariously obsessive masturbator who introduced me to some interesting things I want to try out *cough* like attempt to get an "O" while working out.<br><br>Even after taking herself back to the top with her super successful PR firm she is still a little scared girl under all that "armor" who need some TLC... enter <i>Big Daddy</i><b> - Warner Truman</b> (now I know some may cringe from that title but I flipping love it... so ignore that part if you dare but I'm sticking to Big Daddy Title.)<br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.com/i/f5tumblrinlinemfgm9jl9qn1g/" rel="nofollow noopener">

Just naughty enough and I loved that he did not get bulldozed by alpha bitch like Red... because honestly sometimes us New Yorkers need a Big Daddy to calm our asses down and release the control just a TAD! With a heavy hand giving her the pleasure that any girl dreams of this HEA story is amazing... fast paced, dirty to the point of raunchy, but sooo full of heart and TLC. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I can also tell you haven't experienced love. Not in a long time - if ever."<br><br>"No, you're right."<br><br>"You deserve to be loved. Please let me show you." He drew her face to his and kissed her. "I'll show you if you let me."</i>

Thank you for this wonderful ride and can't wait to meet the rest of the characters</i><br><br>PS... thank you for commenting and guiding through the book... it made it all that much better.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432678ra/869381.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and a little bit of this 'cause you been a <s>good</s> naughty girl<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432678ra/869382.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <span id="freeText88892633558104003" style="display:none">Well this is a conundrum if I've ever been in one... Let's see if I can talk my way through figuring out a star rating... <br><br>So being completely honest, I would say through the first 55% of this book or so I just felt kind of... <br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/ummmno.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432457ra/868675.gif" alt=" photo ummmno.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I thought it was well written. There were some funny aspects to it, but I also felt like at times that Taddy was a bit too much. I got her character and later on it made sense why she was so brazen and obsessed with orgasms, masturbation, and fucking anything with a penis but in the first part of the book I just found myself not liking her or really any of the characters all that much. It felt like they were trying too hard to be outrageous. <br><br>Everyone was either all struggling with... <br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/massiveinsecurity.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I wasn't able to connect or sympathize with the characters until much later. I know that's one of my personal hang ups. I am fine with people being rich and extravagant in books don't get me wrong some of my favorite characters are those lovely billionaire alpha's that we tend to run into in trilogies! I guess the counselor/advocate in me sometimes just won't turn off and all I can see is white privilege and first world problems and it makes me feel... <br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/JakeYuck.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432457ra/868678.gif" alt=" photo JakeYuck.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So at this point I was ready to either chuck the book and say okay this just isn't for me and dnf or finish it and just not rate it since I am sure I am in the minority with my feelings for most of the book. The more parts that were narrated by <i>Warner</i> kept me hanging on and I thought okay maybe I'll finish it and give it 3 stars...<br><br>But then we hit the 60%ish mark and low and behold <i>Warner</i> is on his - full on grown man, alpha, killing the vagina, I know what I want and that's you forever status... <br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/untilidie.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432457ra/868680.gif" alt=" photo DROOL.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then I start thinking okay fuck it, let's just forget the first half of this book and ride <s><i>Warners'</i> face</s> the wave until it's done. <br><br>Because <i>Warner</i> was just... <br><br> <a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/hot-as-balls.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_694767832" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/694767832" />
    <a title="Jen " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5962787-jen"><img alt="Jen " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563496869p2/5962787.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/694767832?book_show_action=true">Aug 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen " href="/user/show/5962787-jen">Jen </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=arc-net-galley">arc-net-galley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=made-me-laugh">made-me-laugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=arc-from-author">arc-from-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer694767832" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9517088834773890502"><b>3-3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b><i>”It’s not my intention to be a diva. It just happens. I wake up like I’m flippin’ Beyoncé or something.” - </i>Taddy Brill, CEO of Brill, Inc.</b><br/><br/>I liked but didn’t love <i>Unscrupulous</i> and my 3 star rating represents just that. It was funny and snarky in all the best ways. By the end, though, I wasn’t feeling any real connection to the characters other than a high level of praise for their snarktitude and a certain envy that Taddy was able to get off while at the same time getting in some time </span>
  <span id="freeText9517088834773890502" style="display:none"><b>3-3.5 Stars</b><br /><br /><b><i>”It’s not my intention to be a diva. It just happens. I wake up like I’m flippin’ Beyoncé or something.” - </i>Taddy Brill, CEO of Brill, Inc.</b><br /><br />I liked but didn’t love <i>Unscrupulous</i> and my 3 star rating represents just that. It was funny and snarky in all the best ways. By the end, though, I wasn’t feeling any real connection to the characters other than a high level of praise for their snarktitude and a certain envy that Taddy was able to get off while at the same time getting in some time at the gym.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>”Please do not masturbate while I do your feet. I cannot take another moaning horny white woman this week.”<br /><br />“I adore DILF porn, but not enough to go to Palm Beach. You?” Being mistaken as two young prostitutes strutting Worth Avenue wasn’t stacked in her good-time cards this holiday.</i>
</b><br /><br />Yep, this book was all kinds of fun. Did I mention the snark? I especially enjoyed Taddy’s interactions with her virginal and highly religious assistant, Kiki. I expected Kiki to come off as kind of a wilting flower around Taddy but she held her own nicely.<br /> <br />On the other hand, Taddy relationship with Warner seemed a little stiff and uptight. The writing has an even tone through the entire story so even when something dramatic happens, it still lacks for drama. Not to say I didn’t enjoy it. I did. It’s just that they could’ve been having hot monkey sex against a wall or shopping for shoes and I would’ve felt the same way about both scenes.<br /><br />On to the sex. <b>You know when you get together with your very best male BFF, who also happens to be gay, and you both get drunk and start to write a humorous porno? Please tell me I’m not the only one to have ever done that?</b> The sexy times sort of read like that. Kind of sexy and kind of laugh out loud funny at the same time.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>She dropped her jaw. Shut the front flippin’ door! “Anaconda” wouldn’t do this super-size of beef justice. <br /><br />“What are we going to do about your sex spigot?”<br />“Stop my spout up.”</i>
</b><br /><br />I enjoyed all of the scenes featuring Warner’s giant anaconda, they just didn’t inspire any lusty thoughts. I am going to call foul on one scene that just had me shaking my head in disbelief. Taddy gets so sexually excited by working out on an elliptical and thinking about Warner that she makes herself come while finishing her workout. With her hand. In a gym. Just…NO! After I was done spawning, I lost 60 lbs. of baby weight via elliptical and not once did the thought of getting off in the sexual sense ever cross my mind. I wanted to kick the shit out of it and possibly push it over a cliff, but never once did I get so worked up that I just couldn’t hold off any longer. Working out would be a whole lot more fun if the big O was part of the deal.<br /><br />If you’re in the mood for some serious contemplation and angst, look elsewhere. If you’re looking for some laughs and a good time, give <i>Unscrupulous</i> a shot.<br /><br /><i>ARC provided by the Author via Net Galley in exchange for an honest review</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="9517088834773890502" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14918539696651068121"><b>4 "Forever Red" Stars</b><br/><br/>Let me start by saying that I loved reading this book. It was so refreshing to have both the heroine and the hero being equals. This book reminded me of Sex in the City on steroids-wickedly delicious steroids!! I loved that there were 4 independent, fabulous fierce friends who shared their lives together while living in NYC!! There is something magical about NYC- I only wished that I would have lived there too!!<br/><br/>So, this story is about the lovely, intelligent, take charge, lo</span>
  <span id="freeText14918539696651068121" style="display:none"><b>4 "Forever Red" Stars</b><br><br>Let me start by saying that I loved reading this book. It was so refreshing to have both the heroine and the hero being equals. This book reminded me of Sex in the City on steroids-wickedly delicious steroids!! I loved that there were 4 independent, fabulous fierce friends who shared their lives together while living in NYC!! There is something magical about NYC- I only wished that I would have lived there too!!<br><br>So, this story is about the lovely, intelligent, take charge, loyal to her friends, sexy, fire cracker, and vulnerable Miss Taddy Brill.....<br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Red_zps8762a2e0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432811i/870569._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Red_zps8762a2e0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Taddy and the color Red-<b>"Your passion for life, the confidence you have within you to move forward and the love you give to others and deserve, but never expect in return."</b><br><br>Taddy is a sex demon who isn't afraid of her sexuality. There were so many funny one liners in this book. She says it like she sees it. She makes no excuses for how she is- she is dynamite and a joy to read. Her friends/family are a great group- Lex, Vive and Blake are all sexy, sassy and there for Taddy no matter what!! <br><br>In an unexpected trip to St. Barth's- at one of Warner Truman's hotels, worlds collide, Taddy and Warner meet and sparks ignite. <br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/bigdaddy_zps869f5bae.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432811i/870570._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo bigdaddy_zps869f5bae.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Warner is a gentleman. <b>"May I?"</b> He is confident, romantic, sexy, knows what he wants and loves his nickname "Big Daddy". <br><br>They have an instant connection, in a bar, over champagne.<br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Gifs/Trachtenberg__Euro__027lrg_zpsa383aa6c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432811ra/870571.gif" alt=" photo Trachtenberg__Euro__027lrg_zpsa383aa6c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>Sweet Jesus nipplelicious. He's got me.<br><br>She tripped high on his Big Daddy ecstasy. Being in his arms wasn't a walk through her beloved Central Park. It was a psychedelic journey in Candy Land with a race to her p*ssy castle.<br><br>She'd waited years to sit, talk, stroke and play with a man such as this. Am I shallow? Abso-fucking-lutely! Who cares?</b><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/unscrumptious_zps0bd1da60.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432811i/870572._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo unscrumptious_zps0bd1da60.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This intensity would be derailed and lost. For the next 6 months, Warner searched for Red, thought of Red and ultimately thought he would never see her again. Taddy, had given up relationships for her New Year's Eve resolution with her friends. They would work on their businesses. Even though Taddy worked nonstop, images of Big Daddy haunted her and of what might have been. In a crazy mishap,(involving a porn star- must read to find out more) Warner and Taddy are reunited in Cannes. Their sexual chemistry is right where they had left it and hot damn it is scorching and panty melting!!!<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/white%20collar%20gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432811ra/870573.gif" alt="white collar gifs photo: tumblr_lfz77qolrk1qdz0rco1_500-1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1130.photobucket.com/user/EllyCrysLya/media/SEXY%20COUPLES/46.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432811i/870574._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 46.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/image_zps00488b55.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432812i/870575.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps00488b55.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Taddy and Warner are 2 extremely successful people. They don't need money, they have power, but what they both are in need of is someone to share their life. Warner, is ready and has love it give. Taddy, who never had love shown to her, is scared to commit. <br><br><b>"You deserve to be loved. Please let me show you." He drew her face to his and kissed her. "I'll show you if you let me."</b><br><br>While this is a love story, it is a sassy, sexy, foul mouth good time read!! You will laugh out loud, be happy, blush and enjoy yourself silly while reading. You gotta love a New York Girl. I think if you are not one, you secretly wish you were one. I look forward to reading the rest of The Manhattanites series about Lex, Vive and Blake.<br> <br><b>Manhattanites are noted as a jaded bunch. We own designer footwear in excess, overspend on vodka cocktails and work sunup to sundown. By accident love takes a backseat but we always find time for sex (wink).</b> <br> <br>Thanks to Avery Aster for providing me a copy via NetGallery in exchange for my honest review♥♥</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6108797066276842437"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433362i/872027._SY540_.jpg' width='280' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>DNF at 61 percent.</b><br/><br/>I really want to love all the books that I read. And especially the ones that I get as an ARC. I appreciate all the hard work that's behind a book but I have to be honest and I am very sure that this book couldn't get better for me. There were some light streaks but after I while I quit reading and I still don't want to read anything.<br/><br/><b>So here it goes:</b><br/><br/>1. I had issues with the language. It was to crude for me. The girlfriends were pretty vulgar. I couldn't stand "He's so hung" ove</span>
  <span id="freeText6108797066276842437" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433362i/872027._SY540_.jpg" width="280" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>DNF at 61 percent.</b><br><br>I really want to love all the books that I read. And especially the ones that I get as an ARC. I appreciate all the hard work that's behind a book but I have to be honest and I am very sure that this book couldn't get better for me. There were some light streaks but after I while I quit reading and I still don't want to read anything.<br><br><b>So here it goes:</b><br><br>1. I had issues with the language. It was to crude for me. The girlfriends were pretty vulgar. I couldn't stand "He's so hung" over and over.<br>2. Write what you know. You shouldn't miss on details like champagnes or the airport close to Cannes. And I seriously doubt that two billionaires would act like those two.<br>3. The sex. It wasn't hot at all for me. The language completely ruined it for me.<br>4. It was snarky but not romantic. I couldn't <i>feel</i> it. And as a reference, I adore Sex and the City.<br><br><b>So the bottom line: I think it's a book you either love or hate.</b> It's not bland at all. And many people love it - so you might as well.<br><br><i>Thank you Avery and Netgalley for providing me with an ARC. I am sorry I didn't like it more.</i> </span>

But as hot and delicious as Mr. Warner Truman is, the heart of Unscrupulous is Taddy Brill. <br/><br/>Taddy is young, beautiful, successful and outrageously sexy. She knows what she wants and is not afraid to say exactly what's on her mind. She built herself an empire where she rules as a benevolent, vajazzled queen</span>
  <span id="freeText10080098731011058748" style="display:none"><b>4.5 outrageous, vajazzled stars!!</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/rKKBeXh" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430693i/863607.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Move over, Mr. Cross. There's a new hot billionaire in town! Warner Truman is hot, sexy, gorgeous and loaded. And I mean loaded in every sense of the word. But as hot and delicious as Mr. Warner Truman is, the heart of Unscrupulous is Taddy Brill. <br><br>Taddy is young, beautiful, successful and outrageously sexy. She knows what she wants and is not afraid to say exactly what's on her mind. She built herself an empire where she rules as a benevolent, vajazzled queen. But behind the designer clothes, the gorgeous shoes and the vajazzle lies a vulnerable young woman. I can honestly say that the Taddy's back story had me in tears. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/B91LggO" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430693i/863608.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She's the epitome of poor, little rich girl. But instead of wallowing in self-pity, Taddy grew up to be a self-assured business woman. That is not to say, she doesn't have issues. She does. But she grew up and learned to acknowledge and change them. Taddy was contented with her business and her hot meaningless affairs until she met Warner Truman.<br><br>Warner was the opposite of Taddy in every sense. He had a stable family life and was actually married for a decade until his wife died of cancer. With the death of his wife, he never thought he could fall in love again that is until Taddy of course. <br><br>Their first meeting was a comedy of errors. It was hilarious and hot at the same time. I was giggling the whole time especially when Taddy misheard his name and called him by a sound-alike name the whole time. LOL! I was so embarrassed for her but Warner was such a sweetheart, he just let her call him whatever she wants. ♥♥<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/cucx5jn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430693i/863609.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Unscrupulous equates fun erotica. The humor runs toward the outrageous and raunchy but never tasteless. This is like Sex and City but younger and actually sexier. And as I mentioned before, this book actually had a lot of heart. <br><br>The secondary characters; Lex, the bankrupt designer BFF; Vive, the pill popping, gossip magazine Maven; the virginal assistant, Kiki and Blake, the married gay best friend all contributed to Taddy and Will's story. And you can't help but fall in love with them, flaws and all. I have to tell you though, I am pretty much intrigued by Blake and I'm hoping and praying that Ms. Aster will have a book for him. <br><br><a href="http://s1335.photobucket.com/user/Geri_Anne/media/whoruntheworldgif_zps516c53a7.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430693ra/863610.gif" alt=" photo whoruntheworldgif_zps516c53a7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So if you like to read about girls who run their world, who love their men hung, their money, their sexy shoes and their orgasms, and makes no apologies for it, then this book is for you. If you're looking for the answer to the meaning of life and the order of the universe, then this book isn't for you either. But if you're up for some fun, sexy, hot, outrageous read, then you're in luck because Unscrupulous is the book for you. ♥♥ <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10080098731011058748" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

The characters had nothing to do with, well <b>not </b>completely anyway. It started out <b>really</b> slow for me. That I almost <b>DNF</b> it. But I continued in hopes it would get better. I got Taddy Brill's <b>sad</b> upbringing made her into the person she now is, but in the beginning, Taddy was a bit <b>annoying</b>. The whole first part of the book was a</span>
  <span id="freeText1824206440516110536" style="display:none"><b>~Arc provided by author via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review~</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433334i/871971._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 2.75 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/472805.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am <b>so</b> sorry to say that I didn't enjoy this book as much as I did the first one. The characters had nothing to do with, well <b>not </b>completely anyway. It started out <b>really</b> slow for me. That I almost <b>DNF</b> it. But I continued in hopes it would get better. I got Taddy Brill's <b>sad</b> upbringing made her into the person she now is, but in the beginning, Taddy was a bit <b>annoying</b>. The whole first part of the book was about her wanting <b>this</b> guy's cock and this other guy's cock, pretty much anyone would do, she was that desperate. I was getting <b>overwhelmed</b> with her <b>obsession</b> with sex. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445490529ra/16660532.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So <b>that</b> was the pretty much the first part of the book. I was waiting for <b>a</b> relationship to develop, and <b>all</b> that happened was she met Warner Truman <b>aka "Big Daddy"</b> and it was <b>insta love</b>. They <b>didn't</b> end up sleeping together that night due to someone showing up. I found it a bit hard to believe how <b>quickly</b> their feelings for each other were growing. Especially after <b>not</b> seeing each other for <b>months</b>, but still, they were hung up on that <b>one brief</b> encounter. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404467ra/787065.gif" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Finally</b> it starts going somewhere when around <b>60%</b>, Taddy and Warner meet again. This is when my <b>interest</b> was peaked. The sex was <b>hot</b> and all, but I still was <b>unable</b> to connect with characters. I did love that Warner pushed Taddy's limits and showed her what <b>love</b> is, even if that love developed <b>too</b> fast. <b>Warner</b> was <b>hot</b>, <b>sweet</b>, and <b>swoony</b>. I liked him a lot, I think he was the most <b>interesting</b> character in this book. His back story was also a <b>sad</b> one. He was afraid to love but he took a <b>chance</b> on Taddy. Taddy was <b>a lot</b> better in the second half of the book, again <b>thanks</b> to Big Daddy. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419803769ra/13128882.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The ending was <b>good</b>, but it fell a <b>bit</b> flat for me. I really think that there <b>wasn't </b>enough of chance for the connection that Taddy and Warner shared to <b>flourish</b>. Had there been <b>more</b> of the relationship from the start, I would have <b>enjoyed</b> it more. I <b>wish</b> I could have liked it more, I <b>really</b> tried but I guess it just <b>wasn't</b> for me. It seems some of my <b>GR friends</b> have enjoyed it. So, who knows, <b>you</b> may like it better than <b>I</b> did.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer696305996" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5022339956380379678"><b>2 LET-ME-TELL-YOU-WHY STARS</b><br/><br/><b>Reason #3:</b><br/><br/><b>The plot.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433266ra/871787.gif' alt='image' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ms. Aster, you need a <b>new editor…like, say…ME.</b> If you would have given me this book, I would have given it back to you and said, “This book has no plot.” <br/><br/>And then I would have chopped it in half. But I would also say, “I know you can do better than this.” <br/><br/>There is something inside of you that needs to be <b>exposed,</b> and I’m not talking about your vajayjay. <br/><br/>There is so much <b>potential</b> to a book like this because I can see how unique it could be.<br/><br/>Sure, you’</span>
  <span id="freeText5022339956380379678" style="display:none"><b>2 LET-ME-TELL-YOU-WHY STARS</b><br><br><b>Reason #3:</b><br><br><b>The plot.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433266ra/871787.gif" alt="image" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ms. Aster, you need a <b>new editor…like, say…ME.</b> If you would have given me this book, I would have given it back to you and said, “This book has no plot.” <br><br>And then I would have chopped it in half. But I would also say, “I know you can do better than this.” <br><br>There is something inside of you that needs to be <b>exposed,</b> and I’m not talking about your vajayjay. <br><br>There is so much <b>potential</b> to a book like this because I can see how unique it could be.<br><br>Sure, you’ve got a 4 star average rating on this book, but I know you can do better.<br><br><b>Reason #2:</b><br><br><b>The characters.</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433266ra/871788.gif" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Who are these people?!?</b> Do you know who they are Ms. Aster?? I couldn’t get a picture of them. <br><br>Was Warner hot? Yes. But I’ve read hotter. He was just ok. <br><br>I <b>wanted</b> to love these characters. <br><br>I found myself leaning into my kindle <b>waiting</b> for something amazing to <b>pop</b> out about these characters, but nothing happened.<br><br><b>Reason #1: </b><br><br><b>The feels.</b><br><br><img alt="pththt" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/601030.gif" width="450" height="248" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I didn’t <b>FEEL</b> anything!!!<br> <br>Sure. I get it. This is supposed to be a fun, funny, book. <br><br>But I felt like Ms. Aster <b>wanted</b> me to feel something, whether it be a connection with the friendship between the 3 girlfriends, for the sad pasts of any of the characters…but <b>I wasn’t buying what Ms. Aster was selling. </b><br><br>You don’t have to create crazy drama to get me to feel something. You just need to <b>SELL</b> your story and your characters. Make me like them. <b>Pull me into your head, into your book and don’t let me leave until you let me.</b><br><br>Did I smile? Yes. Did I laugh? Yes. Was the sex hot? Yes. <br><br>I didn’t love it. I didn’t hate it. I was just….<b>ok.</b><br><br><img alt="" width="500" height="255" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412574ra/811342.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>ARC provided by the author via Netgalley for an honest review</i><br></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer693624129" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4952375676998672223">This is tricky, I hate to be negative but this book just wasn't for me. Lots of other people, however, have given it a fabulous rating so please check out their reviews....<br/><br/>♥<i> I have to be honest with my thoughts.......</i><br/><br/>The plot felt disjointed and didn't grab my attention. Tabby had some great lines and there was a lot of sexy times which I always LOVE but, because I wasn't feeling the story, I guess the sex and one liners lost impact for me. It was a little superficial and lacking in depth but th</span>
  <span id="freeText4952375676998672223" style="display:none">This is tricky, I hate to be negative but this book just wasn't for me. Lots of other people, however, have given it a fabulous rating so please check out their reviews....<br><br>♥<i> I have to be honest with my thoughts.......</i><br><br>The plot felt disjointed and didn't grab my attention. Tabby had some great lines and there was a lot of sexy times which I always LOVE but, because I wasn't feeling the story, I guess the sex and one liners lost impact for me. It was a little superficial and lacking in depth but this is only my opinion.<br><br>What I did like was Warner's back story, his history...it was touching and sad and I feel it could have been explored more.....I possibly would have preferred that story......<br><br>Warner's 'history' taught him a very important lesson....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432888i/870736.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Well it doesn't have to be <b>always</b>, but I like the sentiment! lol </i><br><br>I thought Warner had a lot of potential but again I couldn't completely warm to him......his character felt disjointed to me <br><br>I also liked the history behind Tabby.....and the mothers.....it was interesting but again I don't feel it was explored in depth.<br> <br>Tabby seemed quite shallow in many ways...I couldn't get to the heart of her character and so I never really connected with her in anyway which caused major problems for me and my enjoyment of this book. <br><br>****<br><br>I LOVED these quotes from Warner who, in my opinion, was the best part of this story.<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432888i/870737._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Tonight, I want you to come again and again for me." ~ Warner</b><br><i>I love that line ♥<br><br><br>**Thank you to Avery Aster who kindly provided me with an arc of this book via NetGalley</i></span>

</i></span>
  <span id="freeText17929834304948673190" style="display:none"><br /><br />I have to say I stumbled across this Manhattanites series a week or so ago.<br />I saw it on Amazon and all the five star ratings peaked my interest.<br />Also the fact that the stories are supposed to take place in my favorite city!!<br /><br />I had high hopes.<br />I'm still quite STUNNED at all the 4&amp; 5 star reviews on amazon &amp; good reads.<br />Did I read the same book as all these people?<br /><br />The vocabulary in this one was so vulgar and crass.<br />Believe me, I love a good Erotica book but some of the lines in this one had me cringing<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"Milk it. That's it. There you go," he moaned hoarsely. "Get your tongue in my slit, suck me dry."Warner grabbed her as his body trembled violently with one final release. Leaning down and kissing her open mouth, he demanded. "Gimme" What? She shoved her tongue between his lips, pushing his release back.</b>
</i><br /><br />Slits leaking, cunt creaming, etc.<br />Just not what I think of as sexy...yuk!<br /><br />I could not relate to the heroine, Taddy, Red, Princess Lolly, and so forth and so on.<br />The woman is in heat 24/7 and even gets aroused working out on an Elliptical.<br />I've never gotten aroused on an elliptical...never, ever!!<br />I can't even let go of the handle bars for fear of falling off but she manages to play with herself and orgasm!<br />Bravo!!!<br /><br />I at first loved Warner.<br />I thought this guy is gonna save the story for me!!<br />Oh but he failed me!!<br />Warner, Garner, Big Daddy, Mr Ananconda, King of Candy Land.....too many names!!<br />Anyhow he creeped me out during sex with Taddy, he's calling her Baby Girl, and Young Lady.<br />Scolding her in the midst of having sex, it was just really creepy and not a turn on.<br />Add in a couple of times where he yells "WOO HOO" in bed with her and I totally lost the lust for Big Daddy!<br /><br />Omg I'm not even going to go too into the scene with the porn star jacking off outside on the hotel terrace above a huge screaming crowd!! They were actually cheering until they received that unwelcome shower!!<br />Geez, how did that even end up as part of the storyline??<br /><br />I did kind of like the closure Taddy gets with her sorry ass excuse for a mother @ the end of the book.<br /><br />I wish the story focused more on Warner and Taddy.<br />Took too long for the two to connect and then it was like Instant Love between the two after a night of crazy sex.<br />I'm surprised the lady's vagina didn't fall off!!!<br /><br />Yea and I didn't care for her wanting to be hit or choked during.<br />Glad Warner was not down with that either but he did talk too much during sex.<br />Men don't usually carry on a full articulate conversation during the heat of the moment.<br /><br />I'm sorry I truly wish I could agree with all the other reviews here but I can't be dishonest.<br /><br />It's a big accomplishment to put pen to paper and create a story.<br />I'll give Avery some credit.<br />I just feel the sexy time language needs to be sexy and not utterly vulgar, and you need to make a heroine likable or relatable.<br />The male lead needs to be a strong and yet romantic man, not the Chatty Cathy, galavanting around at the ball in a white feathery thong. This reminded me of that movie "54" with Mike Meyers and Ryan Phillipe.<br /><br />All just a bit fruity!!<br />So if you like a book that is pure fluff with a bunch of flamboyant characters who just have plain, dirty sex, then I'd say definitely read this one.<br /><br /><br />*ARC received from Publisher*<br /></span>

  <span id="freeText6302126791361609097" style="display:none">This book has been sitting on my NetGalley shelf for six years and I decided it was time to read it to clean my closet once and for all. I’m sorry to say that maybe it’s been there so long for a good reason. It’s described as a hilarious and naughty erotic romance, but for me it was just a painful waste of an evening. I’m sure there are others who enjoyed this as evidenced by the many four and five star reviews, but this book was not for me. I had to DNF about two-thirds of the way through and gave it one star. I thank NetGalley for the opportunity to read it.</span>

<div id="review_692693759" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/692693759" />
    <a title="Claire Robinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14026987-claire-robinson"><img alt="Claire Robinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431471072p2/14026987.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/692693759?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Claire Robinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Claire Robinson" href="/user/show/14026987-claire-robinson">Claire Robinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692693759" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14468966726734631302">Avery Aster has done it again. <br/><br/>When I finished reading Undressed, I didn’t think I could be more surprised, shocked or completely and utterly hands-down, jaw droppingly blown away at the erotic creativity of this lady, I was wrong. <br/><br/>She has an impressive ability of being able to describe people, situations, and general locations in vivid, colourful full HD detail. She also borders on genius with her dirty mind and unique view on erotica writing. I have never come across another author who can pac</span>
  <span id="freeText14468966726734631302" style="display:none">Avery Aster has done it again. <br /><br />When I finished reading Undressed, I didn’t think I could be more surprised, shocked or completely and utterly hands-down, jaw droppingly blown away at the erotic creativity of this lady, I was wrong. <br /><br />She has an impressive ability of being able to describe people, situations, and general locations in vivid, colourful full HD detail. She also borders on genius with her dirty mind and unique view on erotica writing. I have never come across another author who can pace a novel so fast, but at the same time leaves nothing out, or feeling as if it has been rushed. The exploits of Lex and Massimo in Undressed left me laughing my socks off, and I am not ashamed to admit squirming a little myself in parts, Warner and Taddy go one step further and what a great step it is.<br /><br />The emotion in this book is stronger, it is still full of the sharp conversation, and witty retorts that Avery is soooo good at, but you really feel there is more going on between this couple and I loved it.<br /><br />Both bear the emotional scars of past hurts, but neither are afraid to look at them, and tackle them head on for the chance of a full relationship with each other. Both characters are strong independent people, I liked that a lot as it is quite unusual to see this in today’s fiction (particularly erotic).<br /><br />This series is in your face, unapologetically hot, its hard, fast, soft and sweet, and all of degrees in-between. Some may be concerned that such a recipe wouldn’t work, but it does and well. <br /><br />Oh and if you’re not sure what a Vajazzle is, find out somewhere out of the public eye. Luckily they are pretty normal in the UK <br /><br /><br /></span>

          </span>

    <a title="Sierra McBride" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6953445-sierra-mcbride"><img alt="Sierra McBride" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421851308p2/6953445.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/695949022?book_show_action=true">Aug 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sierra McBride" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sierra McBride" href="/user/show/6953445-sierra-mcbride">Sierra McBride</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17453515-unscrupulous">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6953445-sierra-mcbride?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6953445-sierra-mcbride?shelf=series-incomplete">series-incomplete</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6953445-sierra-mcbride?shelf=bad-boy">bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6953445-sierra-mcbride?shelf=rich-famous-hero">rich-famous-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6953445-sierra-mcbride?shelf=arrogant-hero">arrogant-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6953445-sierra-mcbride?shelf=series-hea">series-hea</a>
          </div>
