        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer695949022" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer311456387111878493"><b>3-3.5 Stars.</b><br/><br/>I`m going to attempt to put my jumbled ass thoughts together. : )<br/>There is no need to waste space and type a synopsis. Check above !<br/><br/><br/><b>The Good.</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"We have a problem... a whopper to be exact." Taddy heaved her breasts out. She loved scaring the flat-chested new hires with her knockers."</b>
</i><br/><br/>The story was light. I love dark romance, but sometimes you just need something normal. This was that story. Taddy is a somewhat normal girl, with insecurities, although she doesn`t let them show much. I </span>
  <span id="freeText311456387111878493" style="display:none"><b>3-3.5 Stars.</b><br /><br />I`m going to attempt to put my jumbled ass thoughts together. : )<br />There is no need to waste space and type a synopsis. Check above !<br /><br /><br /><b>The Good.</b><br /><br /><i>
  <b>"We have a problem... a whopper to be exact." Taddy heaved her breasts out. She loved scaring the flat-chested new hires with her knockers."</b>
</i><br /><br />The story was light. I love dark romance, but sometimes you just need something normal. This was that story. Taddy is a somewhat normal girl, with insecurities, although she doesn`t let them show much. I loved that she was blunt and unapologetic. She said what she thought and didn`t second guess herself. She worked hard, not letting anyone get in her way of what she wanted to accomplish. She also owned her sexuality.She was hilarious !<br /><br />Avery Aster has an amazing voice. A voice that can empower women to be themselves and not hide behind their own insecurities. So many women get lost in their everyday lives, work, children, etc. But she paints her heroine as a regular woman, flawed but not excessively so. She doesn`t let her problems/flaws deter her in anyway. That`s what I love about this heroine. She has no shame. It has been so long since I have seen a heroine with these traits. Very refreshing.<br /><br />Taddy`s views on crying. This is for all of those whiny heroines.<br /><i>
  <b>"Girl, dig your acrylics into your palms, bite the inside of your cheek, take a deep breath and suck it up."</b>
</i><br /><br />And the Manuel ferrara reference. If you do not know of this man I suggest you Google him immediately. He is also the only man I watch. Shh .. Don`t tell my hubby, he might get a little jealous if he knows I have a favorite. ; )<br /><br />Warner is amazingly beautiful. Very intelligent as well, can`t get any better than that. He speaks what is on his mind, and doesn`t like to beat around the bush. He expects honesty, as that is what he gives. He knows exactly what he wants. He doesn`t flaunt his wealth, which would be a total turn off. He also talks dirty and says all of the right things. Everything about him is a turn on.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"He was epic from head to toe and back to his other head."</b>
</i><br /><br /><i>
  <b>"You`d like the champagne`s body to sparkle, sense initial firmness as it fills your mouth and experience a cream rush as you swallow."</b>
</i><br /><br /><br /><br /><b>The Bad.</b><br /><br />Taddy is described as having looks similar to a swim suit model, but she sometimes seems so darn desperate. I don`t like that at all. It`s a bit contradictory. Having such good looks should not make her so desperate. If she is willing to sleep with the hired help, why can`t she go out and have a one nighter with some random at a club, if she has such good looks? Doesn`t make any sense.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"She appreciated his talents for washing her whites and didn`t want to mix his business with her pleasure by letting him lick her clitoris. The last time she`d tried to sleep with her domestic staff they`d sued her for sexual harassment."</b>
</i><br /><br />HATED the scene with her masterbating in the pedicure chair and coming onto the pedicurist. It was disgusting really. He got offended and she said, "Oh sorry. It just feels so good." WOW.<br /><br /><br />Okay now my biggest problem. <b>The sex scenes.</b> In an Erotica, the sex scenes are what make the book, usually. This book didn`t have a big plot so the sex scenes were what the reader were looking forward too. This book flopped.<br /><br />We have to wait more than half the book for their first intercourse. Which I had no problem with. But, when it came, I wanted to stop reading. That scene was the one that was supposed to make the reader see that they were meant to be, that they were developing feelings for one another. That didn`t happen. There was no connection whatsoever. Taddy being snarky and whitty in her head? No.<br />For the scene to fall flat and me not being able to feel the connection was disappointing. I mean he`s "hammering into her" and she is thinking about her assistant/friend. That really took away a lot for me. I just couldn`t feel it. Definitely didn`t flow. During the whole scene he is doing his thing, and he has a HUGE cock btw, So he`s doing it good. but here taddy lays taking it but not making a peep. I like my sex scenes to be realistic- moaning, groaning, panting. I didn`t get any of that though. So I didn`t feel anything in return. He can`t be that good if she can`t keep her mind on the task at hand. Especially a task with a man like him.<br />During this 4 page long scene, with how it is worded/written, I`m imagining her lying there doing nothing. That is not sexy or intimate in my opinion. She seems cold and detached, but the writer is telling you to feel otherwise.<br />And the first time anal with the "horse cock" would cause one to scream. It would not be as easy as portrayed in this book. The only thing she said when he penetrated her was, "it burns." <b>NO. WAY.</b> For the first time it is almost impossible, especially with the little prep he did give her. Way too unrealistic for me. <br />It was just terrible. I hate saying that. Truly. But I have to be honest.<br /><br />Cunt I can do, but <i>muff?</i> NO ! Clit is fine, but <i>kernel?</i> NO ! How in the world could that be considered hot? WTF? "Oh baby let me lick your kernel !" UGH.<br /><br />And.. No sexy billionaire should ever say, "WOO-HOO, I L-O-V-E you and I love it when you`re soaked for me." Soaked? Yes. Woo-Hoo? NO !<br /><br /><br />This book just fell flat for me. I loved the snark and banter. But the love just wasn`t there, and that`s what I wanted. Instead of the writer showing you the connection she just told you what it was. I wouldn`t recommend this to anyone that wants an amazing love story with angst. I would reccomend if you want some laughs though. : )<br /><br /><i>ARC provided by the Author via Net Galley in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

Taddy Brill aka Red is abandoned by her parents at a young age and always feels as if she isn't good enough and was just thrown away. She is desperate for love, but avoids intimacy. <div id="review_1384886183" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1384886183" />
    <a title="Sabrina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18085807-sabrina"><img alt="Sabrina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1392065462p2/18085807.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1384886183?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sabrina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sabrina" href="/user/show/18085807-sabrina">Sabrina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25679350-unscrupulous">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18085807-sabrina?shelf=crazy-rich">crazy-rich</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1384886183" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3533587982907530649"><b>2 <i>meh</i> Stars</b><br/><br/>Taddy Brill goes on a New Years trip with her very best friends when she meets Warner Truman. A misunderstanding cuts their night short and she goes back home to New York, leaving Warner wondering who she was. Months later they meet up again when Taddy's assistant is arrested for trespassing at one of Warner's hotel's. He makes a deal with her and drops the charges against her assistant if she spends the night with him. Warner is all in and ready to start something real with her, but </span>
  <span id="freeText3533587982907530649" style="display:none"><b>2 <i>meh</i> Stars</b><br><br>Taddy Brill goes on a New Years trip with her very best friends when she meets Warner Truman. A misunderstanding cuts their night short and she goes back home to New York, leaving Warner wondering who she was. Months later they meet up again when Taddy's assistant is arrested for trespassing at one of Warner's hotel's. He makes a deal with her and drops the charges against her assistant if she spends the night with him. Warner is all in and ready to start something real with her, but Taddy doesn't do relationships and needs some help in that department. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400257871ra/9656331.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I didn't hate this book, but I also didn't like. I skimmed for most of it because I was just bored. It was supposed to be a fun and humorous book and I was looking forward to that, but none of the humor was for me. Well, I guess that's a lie. I had to laugh at how ridiculous the sexy times were.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"What are we going to do about your sex spigot?"<br>"Stop my spout up."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438393296ra/15701995.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Taddy didn't make me laugh, she made me want to punch her obnoxious ass. I may not have hated the book, but I sure did hate her character. She was so vain and spoiled and I just couldn't handle it. I should have realized from the very beginning when she was talking about her employee's and then saying she would have her assistant get a boob job. <br><br>I didn't really have any feelings about Warner because he was barely in the book. We learned the very basics about him but that was it and then what we learned was never explored. Most of the book was just Taddy and her "Manhatinites" so I wanted more of him. I think I would have liked the book more if there was more interaction between Taddy and Warner.<br><br>P.S. Big Daddy? Just no. Okay? NO!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3533587982907530649" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5408262-barbara?shelf=books-with-beautiful-covers">books-with-beautiful-covers</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5408262-barbara?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer815948913" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15036389430576896446"><i>**ARC kindly provided by author via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review**</i><br/><br/>5 STARS!<br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380387693ra/747868.gif' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I was hooked from the first sentence! I don't remember the last time when I had so much fun reading a book.<br/><br/><b>RED</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389479085i/8033597._SY540_.jpg' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>At the age of 13 Tabitha Adelaide „Taddy“ was sent to boarding school, because her mother chose her husband over her daughter. They got rid of her. <b>Dirty secret alert!</b> Oh, how I enjoy these stuff! However, you'll have to read the book to find out since I'm going to keep my mouths closed on that matte</span>
  <span id="freeText15036389430576896446" style="display:none"><i>**ARC kindly provided by author via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review**</i><br><br>5 STARS!<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380387693ra/747868.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was hooked from the first sentence! I don't remember the last time when I had so much fun reading a book.<br><br><b>RED</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389479085i/8033597._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At the age of 13 Tabitha Adelaide „Taddy“ was sent to boarding school, because her mother chose her husband over her daughter. They got rid of her. <b>Dirty secret alert!</b> Oh, how I enjoy these stuff! However, you'll have to read the book to find out since I'm going to keep my mouths closed on that matter :) Taddy became emancipated from her parents at 16 years. Emotionally fragile girl very quickly grew tough and fierce, founded her own company Brill, Inc., shut down her emotions and became unscrupulous in her actions to get whatever she wants from life. From the outside her life seemed fabulous and glamorous, Taddy was super-rich, witty, sharp tongued, stunning and very successful businesswoman with an amazing and supporting friends, but she never got over abandonment. Her favorite color was red, color of passion, strength and power. She gave her love freely to other people not expecting nothing in return. Loving someone was never an option for her, that was a risk she wasn't willing to take.<br> Her past hunted her and her life credo was: „I never meet men with any expectations other than having a good time. Then I’m never disappointed.“ That was so sad. She never felt loved and nobody has ever said those three magic words, we all crave to hear, to my poor Taddy, until she met Him!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389479085ra/8033598.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With her money she bought <i>127 scarves, 249 wraps, 341 hats, 495 gloves, 681 sunglasses, 759 belts, 989 handbags, 1,092 rings, 1,217 pairs of shoes, 1,355 necklaces, and 3,512 pairs of earrings.</i> Dear Lord!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389479085ra/8033599.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, I was a bit jealous, but not too much, because I know the whole story and I wouldn't trade my place with her. Well, maybe for Big Daddy I will reconsider doing it. *evil grins*<br><br><i>„Money always turned her on. Not other people’s cash, just hers, and it was all Brill, Inc.’s.“<br><br>„Waris Sugar, you’re preventing me from getting laid. Turn down this flippin’ music.“<br><br>„She’d waited years to sit, talk, stroke and play with a man such as this.Am I shallow? Abso-fucking-lutely! Who cares?“<br><br>„She tripped high on his Big Daddy ecstasy. Being in his arms wasn’t a walk through her beloved Central Park. It was a psychedelic journey in Candy Land with a race to her pussy castle.“</i><br><br>Hahhahahah, you gotta love her naughty thoughts!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380385031ra/743863.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Taddy was a great heroine to read about, she always spoke her mind, her inner monologues were comical, and not forget to mention her wild fantasies, enormous porn collection, obsession with Brayden Brooks, pleasure room with BDSM equipment and her hilarious efforts to help her Mormon assistant to get rid of her virginity. <br><br><b>BIG DADDY</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389479085i/8033600.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Unlike Taddy, he was raised in loving home and wasn't terrified of intimacy. He was happily married to Josephine for ten years before she had died. She teached him that woman always comes first. <b>Oh, God bless you!</b> Being dirty rich, Warner was constant target of many gold diggers. He almost marry one, luckily he found out the truth before it was too late thanks to her stupid mistake when she had attempted to screw his brother. Yeah, you failed bitch!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/549397.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>„If I ever fall for a woman again, she’ll have her own money.”</i><br><br>Poor guy was already sick and tired of all those attention craving money-whores. Luckily, destiny brought Taddy to him as an award for all that suffering he has been through. She was his perfect match, but boy, did he has to work to his ass off to get to her. Her walls were up and it took him a lot of efforts to get close to her and convince her to give them a chance they both deserved. <br><br><i>„He found a perverse pleasure in her independence. In the past, his girlfriends had jumped at the chance to drop everything and follow him around the world. Not Taddy. He’d finally met his match.“<br><br>„He figured Taddy was similar to a man in the way that to get her attention he’d have to use sex.“</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389479085ra/8033601.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, I really enjoyed reading this book. I didn't expect it to be this good. Wow! Now I definitely need to check the other books from this series. Big thumbs up!</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/685229990" />
    <a title="Linda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5403981-linda"><img alt="Linda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1413068219p2/5403981.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/685229990?book_show_action=true">Aug 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Linda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Linda" href="/user/show/5403981-linda">Linda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5403981-linda?shelf=kindle-books">kindle-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5403981-linda?shelf=challenge-2013">challenge-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5403981-linda?shelf=net-galley">net-galley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5403981-linda?shelf=challenge">challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5403981-linda?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer685229990" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10540985827658233721">Book courtesy of Net Galley and Ellora's Cave !<br/><br/>Great read !<br/><br/>Witty, sexy,ballsy, charming, dominant.. All of these describe any one of the characters in this book and it made me love them even more.<br/>Taddy Brill is a young successful owner and PR rep of her own firm, and poised for world domination, with offices in Times Square, and her best friends Vive, Lex and Blake at her side , she can not miss.<br/>Oh and we can not forget Kiki, her very young , naive, virginal Morman assistant!<br/>Taddy is from an upp</span>
  <span id="freeText10540985827658233721" style="display:none">Book courtesy of Net Galley and Ellora's Cave !<br><br>Great read !<br><br>Witty, sexy,ballsy, charming, dominant.. All of these describe any one of the characters in this book and it made me love them even more.<br>Taddy Brill is a young successful owner and PR rep of her own firm, and poised for world domination, with offices in Times Square, and her best friends Vive, Lex and Blake at her side , she can not miss.<br>Oh and we can not forget Kiki, her very young , naive, virginal Morman assistant!<br>Taddy is from an upperclass well known family, who well for lack of better words on my part; has treated Taddy like shit, sent her off to boarding school and never looked back; everything Taddy has is because she has worked for it.<br> <br>For all of Taddy's success, thanks to her family real relationships are an issue, sure she dates, well one night stands and she is in control, never loosing control of her emotions; tll she meets Warner Truman, successful billionaire hotel and spa mogul. <br>Now, you would think that being Warner owns the hotel in Times Square across the street from Taddy's office and they travel in the same circles they would have met before, but no. Taddy heads to St Bart's will her girlfriends for a getaway and meets Warner quite by accident at one of his clubs attached to his hotel and spa in St Bart's. For the two of them the chemistry is immediate and the encounter hot as hell, but what starts off promising tanks really fast.<br> Taddy will not encounter Warner again for months, months of working non stop, building her empire, no men no sex and invading thoughts of him. What is that, oh how do they wind up together again you ask? Good question. Taddy has to fly to Caanes to bail out Kiki , yes , you remember Kiki the virginal Morman assistant, seems she was arrested for well a little something to do with pornography , but. I digress, besides the author tells so much better than I ever could.<br>Needless to say , it turns out this all happened at one of Warner's properties, so to get Kiki charges dropped Taddy trades her PR expertise and her time . Warner , who has not been able to get Taddy off his mind has just hit the jackpot.<br><br>Well, I think Taddy has too, because sex with Warner is incredible and for Taddy frightening because Warner wants the emotional connection ; and thanks to her family emotional is a challenge . Warner is patient, loving, supportive and committed to making this relationship work and the sex is like nothing she has had before. <br><br>So have I told you enough plot line yet? I think so!<br>Great read, great characters and soooooo....... Looking forward to the next book, next up Blake's story.<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17453516.Unsaid__The_Manhattanites___3_" title="Unsaid (The Manhattanites, #3) by Avery Aster" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1373742156s/17453516.jpg" alt="Unsaid (The Manhattanites, #3) by Avery Aster" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> and I hope more of that delicious Warner , well okay Taddy too!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+VvXphrJOMvA+j+ggmoBZ2ss5dFln4Goyhicn2vhiJw/Cc6gIrGakawNAtH/Iuw0WQXAahpcEUBfUOQIT+USaQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }
